{"ex_id": "test_362", "sentence": "When you're wearing cotton shirts, you're consuming Cellulose.", "label": "true", "entity": "Cellulose", "en_wiki_pageid": "6911", "entity_mention_loc": [[52, 61]], "dpr": [{"id": "kilt:6429615", "title": "Platelet lysate", "text": "Human platelet lysate (or hPL) is a substitute supplement for fetal bovine serum (FBS) in experimental and clinical cell culture. It is a turbid, light-yellow liquid that is obtained from human blood platelets after freeze/thaw cycle(s). {"ex_id": "test_848", "sentence": "All species of firefly emit light to attract a mate.", "label": "false", "entity": "Firefly", "en_wiki_pageid": "60996", "entity_mention_loc": [[15, 22]], "dpr": [{"id": "kilt:15331803", "title": "Firefly", "text": "The Lampyridae are a family of insects in the beetle order Coleoptera with over 2,000 described species. Fireflies produce a \"cold light\", with no infrared or ultraviolet frequencies.
